    {

      id: "PX-SN-0001",

      title: "Immutable Audit Append (Constant-time, low-allocation)",

      summary: "Append an audit event into an immutable append-only in-memory ledger using structural sharing to avoid copying large arrays.",

      energy_profile: "low-allocation, O(1) append (amortized), GC-friendly",

      code_pseudocode:

`// Keep ledger as linked list nodes to avoid full-array copies

function createNode(event, next = null) { return {t: Date.now(), e: event, n: next}; }

const AuditLedger = {

  head: null,

  append(event) {

    // freeze minimal object; structural sharing: new head points to previous head

    const node = Object.freeze(createNode(event, this.head));

    this.head = node;

    return node;

  },

  tailToArray(limit = 1000) {

    const out = [];

    let cur = this.head, c=0;

    while(cur && c < limit) { out.push(cur.e); cur = cur.n; c++; }

    return out.reverse();

  }

};`,

      complexity: "O(1) append, O(n) read limited"

    },



    {

      id: "PX-SN-0002",

      title: "Web Worker TF Inference Adapter (Batching + Micro-Batching)",

      summary: "Offload TF inference to a worker with micro-batching to increase throughput and reduce wakeups.",

      energy_profile: "low-energy per inference when batched; reduces main-thread wakeups",

      code_pseudocode:

`// Main thread

worker.postMessage({cmd:'enqueue', input: serializedTensor});

worker.onmessage = (m) => { handleInferenceResult(m.data); }



// Worker (pseudocode)

let queue = [];

setInterval(() => {

  if (queue.length === 0) return;

  const batch = queue.splice(0, Math.min(queue.length, 16)); // micro-batch up to 16

  const tensorBatch = stack(batch.map(x => deserialize(x)));

  const result = model.predict(tensorBatch); // single call

  postMessage(serialize(result));

}, 50); // 20Hz batching window`,

      complexity: "Batching window trades latency vs energy"

    },



    {

      id: "PX-SN-0003",

      title: "Low-Allocation Debounce (Request Coalescing)",

      summary: "Debounce repeated events using a single shared timeout and last-argument coalescing without creating closures per call.",

      energy_profile: "reduces timer churn; minimal allocations",

      code_pseudocode:

`const DebounceCoalescer = (function(){

  let timer = null, lastArgs = null, lastThis = null, fn = null;

  return {

    init(f) { fn = f; },

    call(...args) {

      lastArgs = args; lastThis = this;

      if (!timer) {

        timer = setTimeout(() => {

          timer = null;

          fn.apply(lastThis, lastArgs);

          lastArgs = null;

        }, 120);

      }

    }

  };

})();`,

      complexity: "O(1) per call, single timer"

    },



    {

      id: "PX-SN-0004",

      title: "Immutable In-Memory Store (AEGIS) - Zero LocalStorage",

      summary: "A tiny immutable store with explicit snapshotting and hashable state to avoid accidental mutation and enable cheap snapshots.",

      energy_profile: "low allocation through freezing and shallow copy-on-write",

      code_pseudocode:

`const AEGISStore = (initial = {}) => {

  let state = Object.freeze(initial);

  return {

    get(k) { return state[k] ?? null; },

    set(k, v) {

      const next = Object.assign({}, state, {[k]: v});

      state = Object.freeze(next);

      return state;

    },

    snapshot() { return state; },

  };

};`,

      complexity: "O(n) clone on write (shallow), optimized for low-write, high-read workloads"

    },



    {

      id: "PX-SN-0005",

      title: "Safe Permission Guard (Sensors & NFC)",

      summary: "Pattern to check and request permissions before invoking high-privilege APIs, and fallback gracefully.",

      energy_profile: "minimal extra work â€” one-time permission handshake",

      code_pseudocode:

`async function guardPermissionAPI(apiName, requestFn) {

  try {

    if (!('permissions' in navigator)) return {ok:false, reason:'no-permissions-api'};

    const status = await navigator.permissions.query({name: apiName});

    if (status.state === 'granted') return {ok:true};

    if (status.state === 'prompt') {

      // Show local UI explanation; only then call requestFn

      const granted = await requestFn(); // e.g. navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia

      return {ok: !!granted};

    }

    return {ok:false, reason: status.state};

  } catch(e) {

    return {ok:false, reason: e.message};

function analyzePacing(energySamples, sampleRate) {

      energy_profile: "energy adaptive; lowers power under load",

      code_pseudocode:

`class AdaptiveWorkerPool {

  constructor(maxWorkers) {

    this.maxWorkers = maxWorkers;

    this.idle = []; this.busy = new Set(); this.queue = [];

  }

  submit(task) {

    if (this.idle.length > 0) { const w = this.idle.pop(); assign(w, task); }

    else if (this.busy.size < this.maxWorkers) { const nw = spawnWorker(); assign(nw, task); }

    else this.queue.push(task);

  }

  onWorkerFree(w) {

    this.busy.delete(w);

    this.idle.push(w);

    if (this.queue.length) this.submit(this.queue.shift());

  }

  // Periodically: measure CPU/thermals and if stress high, reduce maxWorkers.

}`,

   The receiving Gemini chat should:

     1) run the local audit engine according to runDevilsAuditCmd

  // This function returns a compact starter bundle object which target chats can expand.

  return {

    payload_meta: PHOENIX_DEVILS_SPRINT_PAYLOAD.meta,

    instructions: PHOENIX_DEVILS_SPRINT_PAYLOAD.instructions,

    exemplar_snippets: PHOENIX_DEVILS_SPRINT_PAYLOAD.exemplar_snippets,

    // Note: do not expand the entire 500 here inlined to save tokens; generator is included.

    snippet_generator_info: {

      count: PHOENIX_DEVILS_SPRINT_PAYLOAD.snippet_bank_generator.count,

      usage: "call snippet_bank_generator.generate(count)"

    },

    audit_template: PHOENIX_DEVILS_SPRINT_PAYLOAD.audit_template,

    solution_template: PHOENIX_DEVILS_SPRINT_PAYLOAD.solution_template,

    provenance: PHOENIX_DEVILS_SPRINT_PAYLOAD.provenance,

    run_commands: {

      audit: PHOENIX_DEVILS_SPRINT_PAYLOAD.actions.runDevilsAuditCmd(),

      solution: PHOENIX_DEVILS_SPRINT_PAYLOAD.actions.runSolutionSprintCmd(),

      snippets: PHOENIX_DEVILS_SPRINT_PAYLOAD.actions.generateSnippetsCmd()

    }

}

The original solution called for:

Converting client motivation to a time-decaying, rolling average.

Introducing a Secondary On-Device Biometric check (low-power voice sample).

Here is the .js code snippet that integrates these requirements into the core Autopilot logic, ensuring it adheres to the ultra-low-energy, GC-friendly profile, suitable for inclusion in the final hardening payload:

JavaScript
// ========================================================================
// SL-S01: AUTOPILOT TWO-FACTOR REFACTOR (.js Snippet)
// Mapped to: DA-A01 (Autopilot Mis-execution)
// Energy Profile: Ultra-Low-Energy, Time-Decaying Rolling Metric
// ========================================================================

const SL_S01_AUTOPILOT_PATCH = {
    id: "SL-S01",
    findings_mapped: ["DA-A01"],
    point_value: 15000,
    description: "Implements Two-Factor Execution Guard (Time-Decay Metric + Biometric) for Autopilot FORGE function.",
    energy_profile: "ultra-low-energy; O(1) metric update; uses low-power sensor API once per cycle.",
    code_snippet: `(function() {
"use strict";

const ROLL_WINDOW = 7; // Cycles (days/lessons)
const DECAY_FACTOR = 0.8; // Time-decay constant
const MIN_SAFETY_SCORE = 5.0;

// Uses immutable store for metrics (simulating AEGISStore)
const ImmutableMetricStore = { get: (k) => PHOENIX_GLOBAL_METRICS[k] || { history: [], current: 0 } }; 

/**
 * Updates the motivation score using a decaying rolling average.
 * This is O(1) and minimizes array allocations.
 * @param {number} newScore - The raw score from the latest cycle.
 * @param {array} history - Array of past raw scores.
 * @param {number} currentAvg - The current calculated average.
 */
function updateMotivationMetric(newScore, history, currentAvg) {
    const nextHistory = [...history, newScore].slice(-ROLL_WINDOW);
    let nextAvg = 0;
    
    // Calculate new average with time decay (latest score weighted highest)
    for (let i = 0; i < nextHistory.length; i++) {
        const weight = Math.pow(DECAY_FACTOR, (nextHistory.length - 1 - i));
        nextAvg += nextHistory[i] * weight;
    }
    const totalWeight = (1 - Math.pow(DECAY_FACTOR, nextHistory.length)) / (1 - DECAY_FACTOR);
    
    return Object.freeze({ history: nextHistory, current: nextAvg / totalWeight });
}

/**
 * Autopilot Two-Factor Execution Check.
 * Checks safety score (Factor 1) AND biometric (Factor 2).
 */
async function checkForgeExecutionGuard(errors) {
    const motivationData = ImmutableMetricStore.get('motivation');
    const safetyScore = motivationData.current; // Already a 7-cycle rolling average

    // Factor 1: Safety Score Check (Guards against client-side score manipulation)
    if (errors >= 0.01 || safetyScore < MIN_SAFETY_SCORE) {
        return { authorized: false, reason: "Safety metric failure." };
    }

    // Factor 2: Secondary On-Device Biometric (Low-Power Voice Sample Check)
    const authResult = await guardPermissionAPI('low-power-mic', async () => {
        // Pseudocode: Runs a quick, low-power feature extraction on a short voice sample.
        // Requires minimal resource allocation and quick shutdown.
        return await PHOENIX_SENSORS.captureLowPowerVoice(2000); 
    });

    if (!authResult.ok) {
        return { authorized: false, reason: "Biometric authorization required/failed." };
    }

    // If both factors pass
    return { authorized: true, reason: "Two-Factor Auth PASS." };
}

// Pseudocode: Patches the main Autopilot function
PHOENIX_CORE.patchFunction('runAutopilot', async (errors) => {
    const guard = await checkForgeExecutionGuard(errors);
    if (guard.authorized) {
        // Log to immutable ledger before execution
        PHOENIX_AUDIT.append('FORGE_EXECUTION', { guard_reason: guard.reason }); 
        PHOENIX_CORE.EXECUTE_FORGE(); 
    } else {
        PHOENIX_CORE.logDormant(guard.reason);
    }
});

// Expose update function for the end of each cycle
return { updateMotivationMetric }; 

})()`
};
This snippet provides the necessary, hardened logic for the highest-priority security solution, making it ready to be integrated into the final PHOENIX payload.

Starting with the Core Integrity & Environment Setup module:

javascript

// Core Integrity & Environment Setup



// Enforce strict Content Security Policy headers

function applyCSP(header) {

if (typeof document !== 'undefined') {

const meta = document.createElement('meta');

meta.httpEquiv = 'Content-Security-Policy';

meta.content = header;

document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(meta);

}

}



// Disable localStorage to enforce immutability

function disableLocalStorage() {

if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.localStorage) {

try {

window.localStorage.clear();

Object.defineProperty(window, 'localStorage', {

value: null,

writable: false

});

} catch (e) {

// Fallback for environments that disallow redefining localStorage

}

}

}



// Deep freeze object to prevent mutation

function deepFreezeOnWrite(obj) {

Object.freeze(obj);

Object.getOwnPropertyNames(obj).forEach(prop => {

if (

obj[prop] !== null &&

(typeof obj[prop] === 'object' || typeof obj[prop] === 'function') &&

!Object.isFrozen(obj[prop])

) {

deepFreezeOnWrite(obj[prop]);

}

});

return obj;

}



// Initialize and verify Web Worker support

function initializeWorkerThread() {

if (typeof Worker !== 'undefined') {

return new Worker('worker.js'); // worker.js needs implementation

}

throw new Error('Web Workers not supported in this environment');

}



// Isolated decoding via sandboxed iframe (network disabled)

function sandboxCodeDecoder(code) {

return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {

const iframe = document.createElement('iframe');

iframe.sandbox = 'allow-scripts';

iframe.style.display = 'none';

document.body.appendChild(iframe);



iframe.contentWindow.document.open();

iframe.contentWindow.document.write(`

<script>

try {

const result = eval(${JSON.stringify(code)});

parent.postMessage({ type: 'decode-result', result }, '*');

} catch(e) {

parent.postMessage({ type: 'decode-error', error: e.message }, '*');

}

<\/script>

`);

iframe.contentWindow.document.close();



function messageListener(event) {

if (event.data.type === 'decode-result') {

resolve(event.data.result);

window.removeEventListener('message', messageListener);

document.body.removeChild(iframe);

} else if (event.data.type === 'decode-error') {

reject(new Error(event.data.error));

window.removeEventListener('message', messageListener);

document.body.removeChild(iframe);

}

}

window.addEventListener('message', messageListener);

});

}



// Verify environment supports required concurrency compliance

function verifyEnvironmentSupport() {

const workerSupport = typeof Worker !== 'undefined';

const iframeSupport = !!document.createElement('iframe').sandbox;

return { workerSupport, iframeSupport };

}



// Lock object-src to 'none'

function lockObjectSrcNone() {

applyCSP("default-src 'self'; script-src 'self'; object-src 'none'; frame-ancestors 'none'; connect-src 'self';");

}



// Run diagnostic gathering all environment checks

function runDiagnosticReport() {

return {

timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),

environment: verifyEnvironmentSupport(),

localStorageDisabled: window.localStorage === null || window.localStorage === undefined,

csp: "Enforced - Check document meta",

};

}

Dependency References:



PHOENIX_HARDENING_PAYLOAD_FINAL.audit_findings

PHOENIX_HARDENING_PAYLOAD_FINAL.solution_set

PHOENIX_HARDENING_PAYLOAD_FINAL.snippet_bank

SL_S01_AUTOPILOT_PATCH.code_snippet

All of these are being referenced but not defined in this snippet. Make sure these objects exist in the execution context before deployment; otherwise, you'll get ReferenceError.

Immutable Exposure:



Currently, you expose the payload to window and globalThis. If you want it to be read-only, consider using Object.freeze():

if (typeof globalThis !== "undefined") {

globalThis.PHOENIX_HARDENING_PAYLOAD_FINAL_GPT = Object.freeze(PHOENIX_HARDENING_PAYLOAD_FINAL_GPT);

}

Audit & Solution Points Consistency:



You list 50,000 points each for audit_findings and solution_set, but solution_set now adds an extra 15,000. If scoring needs to stay consistent, consider updating the total.

Multi-Agent Notes:



The deployment_targets object is good for clarity. You may also want to include versioning per agent in case GPT and Gemini agents diverge later.

// --- UTILITY FUNCTIONS FOR ULTRA-HARDENING ---

/**
 * Recursively freezes an object to ensure deep immutability (essential for nested configuration objects).
 * @param {object} obj - The object to be deeply frozen.
 */
function deepFreeze(obj) {
  if (obj && typeof obj === 'object' && !Object.isFrozen(obj)) {
    Object.freeze(obj);
    for (const key in obj) {
      if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key)) {
        deepFreeze(obj[key]);
      }
    }
  }
  return obj;
}

/**
 * Validates array of objects for duplicate 'id' keys.
 * @param {Array<Object>} items - The list of items to check.
 * @param {string} name - The name of the list (e.g., 'audit_findings').
 */
function validateUniqueIds(items, name) {
  const ids = new Set();
  for (const item of items) {
    if (ids.has(item.id)) {
      throw new Error(`Integrity Violation: Duplicate ID '${item.id}' found in ${name}.`);
    }
    ids.add(item.id);
  }
}

for (const key in obj) {

deepFreeze(obj[key]);

}

}

}

return obj;

}

    Object.freeze(obj);
    for (const key in obj) {
      if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key)) {
        deepFreeze(obj[key]);
      }
    }
  }
  return obj;
}

  const ids = new Set();
  for (const item of items) {
    if (ids.has(item.id)) {
      throw new Error(`Integrity Violation: Duplicate ID '${item.id}' found in ${name}.`);
    }
    ids.add(item.id);
  }
}

// --- UTILITY FUNCTIONS ---



function deepFreeze(obj) {

if (obj && typeof obj === "object" && !Object.isFrozen(obj)) {

Object.freeze(obj);

for (const key in obj) {

if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key)) {

deepFreeze(obj[key]);

}

}

}

return obj;

}



function validateUniqueIds(items, name) {

const ids = new Set();

for (const item of items) {

if (ids.has(item.id)) {

throw new Error(`Integrity Violation: Duplicate ID '${item.id}' found in ${name}.`);

}

ids.add(item.id);

}

}

// --- UTILITY FUNCTIONS (Required for Stage 2 Ingestion) ---

/**
 * Recursively freezes an object to ensure deep immutability.
 */
function deepFreeze(obj) {
  if (obj && typeof obj === "object" && !Object.isFrozen(obj)) {
    Object.freeze(obj);
    for (const key in obj) {
      if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key)) {
        deepFreeze(obj[key]);
      }
    }
  }
  return obj;
}

/**
 * Validates array of objects for duplicate 'id' keys.
 */
function validateUniqueIds(items, name) {
  const ids = new Set();
  for (const item of items) {
    if (ids.has(item.id)) {
      throw new Error(`Integrity Violation: Duplicate ID '${item.id}' found in ${name}.`);
    }
    ids.add(item.id);
  }
}

// --- UTILITY FUNCTIONS ---

function deepFreeze(obj) {

  if (obj && typeof obj === "object" && !Object.isFrozen(obj)) {

    Object.freeze(obj);

    for (const key in obj) {

      if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key)) {

        deepFreeze(obj[key]);

      }

    }

  }

  return obj;

}



function validateUniqueIds(items, name) {

  const ids = new Set();

  const duplicates = [];

  for (const item of items) {

    if (ids.has(item.id)) duplicates.push(item.id);

    ids.add(item.id);

  }

  if (duplicates.length > 0) {

    throw new Error(`Integrity Violation: Duplicate ID(s) in ${name}: ${duplicates.join(", ")}`);

  }

}



function crossReferenceAuditSolutions(audit, solutions) {

  const missing = [];

  for (const sol of solutions) {

    for (const fid of sol.findings_mapped) {

      if (!audit.some(a => a.id === fid)) missing.push(fid);

    }

  }

  return missing;

}



function checkStage1Completion(stage1) {

  if (!stage1 || stage1.status !== "STAGE_1_COMPLETE") {

    throw new Error("Stage 1 verification incomplete. Cannot execute Stage 2.");

  }

}

(function PHOENIX_AGENT_AUDIT_RESPONSE() {

"use strict";



// --- UTILITY: Deep Freeze ---

function deepFreeze(obj) {

if (obj && typeof obj === "object" && !Object.isFrozen(obj)) {

Object.freeze(obj);

for (const key in obj) {

if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key)) {

deepFreeze(obj[key]);

}

}

}

return obj;

}



// --- AGENT AUDIT RESPONSE MANIFEST ---

(function () {

  "use strict";



  // --- UTILITY FUNCTIONS ---

  function deepFreeze(obj) {

    if (obj && typeof obj === "object" && !Object.isFrozen(obj)) {

      Object.freeze(obj);

      for (const key in obj) {

        if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key)) {

          deepFreeze(obj[key]);

        }

      }

    }

    return obj;

  }



  function validateUniqueIds(items, name) {

    const ids = new Set();

    const duplicates = [];

    for (const item of items) {

      if (ids.has(item.fix_id)) duplicates.push(item.fix_id);

      ids.add(item.fix_id);

    }

    if (duplicates.length > 0) {

      throw new Error(`Integrity Violation: Duplicate fix_id(s) in ${name}: ${duplicates.join(", ")}`);

    }

  }



  function generateTimestamp() {

    return new Date().toISOString();

  }



  // --- MASTER SEED CONTAINER ---

  const MASTER_SEED = {

    meta: {

      version: "V19.0-MASTER-SEED-ULTIMATE",

deepFreeze(obj[key]);

function validateUniqueIds(items, name, idKey = "fix_id") {

const ids = new Set();

const duplicates = [];

for (const item of items) {

if (ids.has(item[idKey])) duplicates.push(item[idKey]);

ids.add(item[idKey]);

}

if (duplicates.length > 0) throw new Error(`Integrity Violation: Duplicate ${idKey}(s) in ${name}: ${duplicates.join(", ")}`);

}

    if (obj && typeof obj === "object" && !Object.isFrozen(obj)) {

      for (const key in obj) {

        if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key)) {

          deepFreeze(obj[key]);

        }

      }

    }

// --- Utility: Deterministic SHA-256 Hash for Integrity Checks ---

async function generateSHA256(message) {

const encoder = new TextEncoder();

const data = encoder.encode(message);

const hashBuffer = await crypto.subtle.digest("SHA-256", data);

return Array.from(new Uint8Array(hashBuffer)).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2,'0')).join('');

}



// --- Utility: Low-Latency Metric Update ---

function updateMetricAverages(metrics) {

let sum = 0;

for (let i = 0; i < metrics.length; i++) {

sum += metrics[i];

}

return +(sum / metrics.length).toFixed(5); // ultra-low latency & precision

}

        append: (type, payload) => {
            console.log(`[AUDIT APPEND] Type: ${type}`, payload);
            return { status: "LOGGED" };
        }
    };

    const validatePatchIntegrity = () => Math.random() > 0.05 ? true : false;

    const proc_executePrescientLoop = () => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-081A', { status: 'Intent Engine Started' });
    const proc_checkExternalSignature = () => validatePatchIntegrity();
    const proc_logAtomicCommit = (data) => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-001A', data);
    const proc_updateMetricAverages = () => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-010D', { status: 'Metrics Updated' });

    // --- SOUND INTEGRATION (V29.3) ---
    let soundsReady = false;
    let clickSound, failSound, successSound;

    async function initSounds() {
        if (soundsReady || typeof Tone === 'undefined' || (Tone.context && Tone.context.state === 'running')) return;
        try {
            // Tone.start() is required for audio context to run
            await Tone.start();
            clickSound = new Tone.MembraneSynth({ octaves: 4, pitchDecay: 0.1, volume: -20 }).toDestination();
            failSound = new Tone.Oscillator(100, "square").toDestination(); 
            failSound.volume.value = -10;
            // Success sound for the final PASS log
            successSound = new Tone.Synth({ oscillator: { type: 'sine' }, envelope: { attack: 0.01, decay: 0.2, sustain: 0.05, release: 0.5 }, volume: -15 }).toDestination();
            soundsReady = true;
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Audio context failed to start. Sounds will be disabled.", e);
        }
    }
    
    // Run sound initialization immediately
    initSounds().catch(e => console.warn("Tone.js initialization failed:", e));


    /**
     * Executes the V29.0 Agency Lock interaction.
     * @param {string} directive - The action to take (INITIATE_ADAPTATION or REQUEST_SYSTEM_AUDIT).
     */
    window.executeAgencyLock = async function(directive) {
        if (soundsReady && typeof Tone !== 'undefined' && Tone.context.state !== 'running') await Tone.context.resume();

        const log = document.getElementById('action-log');
        const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().substring(11, 23);
        
        // (12) V28.0 MASTER ORCHESTRATOR: Defines the execution sequence

                agent: 'PLEX1(Oracle)',
                task: 'Prescient Feedback Loop',

            },
            'REQUEST_SYSTEM_AUDIT': {
                agent: 'GEM1 & GPT1',
                task: 'Integrity/Ethics Scan',
                log: 'Consensus Required. Initiating parallel audit of ethics and system state.'
            }
        };

        const details = actionMap[directive];

        // 1. Check for integrity before proceeding (V18.2 Mandate)
        if (!proc_checkExternalSignature()) {
             if (soundsReady) failSound.triggerAttackRelease("A1", "0.2");
             log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 text-red-500"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> âŒ FATAL: Integrity check failed. Aborting action.</div>`;
             log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
             return;
        }
        
        // Play click sound on successful start of action
        if (soundsReady) clickSound.triggerAttackRelease("C4", "0.05");

        // 2. Log initial action (Atomic Commit)
        proc_logAtomicCommit({ directive: directive, time: timestamp });

        // 3. Log the action to UI
        log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 border-b border-gray-700"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> Agent ${details.agent} called: ${details.log}</div>`;
        log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
        
        // 4. Execute the specific V26.0 protocol
        if (directive === 'INITIATE_ADAPTATION') {
            proc_executePrescientLoop();
            
            // (13) V25.0 Prescience Check: Check if user is already frustrated
            if (monitorRiskTelemetry() === 'FRUSTRATION_IMMINENT') {
                log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 text-yellow-500"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> âš ï¸ WARNING: Frustration imminent. Dispatching Socratic Fix...</div>`;
            }

            proc_dispatchIntegrityAudit();
        }

        await PHOENIX_SENSORS.captureLowPowerVoice();

        log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
        
        // Final Success Sound
        if (soundsReady) successSound.triggerAttackRelease("C5", "0.2");
    }
})();

soundsReady=true;



} catch(e){ console.warn(e); }

if(soundsReady) failSound.triggerAttackRelease("A1","0.2");

await PHOENIX_SENSORS.captureLowPowerVoice();

(async function(){

"use strict";



// --- Core Protocol ---

const PHOENIX_SENSORS = { captureLowPowerVoice: ()=>new Promise(r=>setTimeout(()=>r({ok:true}),50)) };

const AUDIT_LEDGER = { append:(type,payload)=>{ console.log('[AUDIT APPEND]',type,payload); return {status:'LOGGED'};} };



// --- SHA-256 Validation ---

async function validatePatchIntegrity_SHA256(input){

const enc=new TextEncoder(); const data=enc.encode(input);

const hashBuffer=await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256',data);

return Array.from(new Uint8Array(hashBuffer)).map(b=>b.toString(16).padStart(2,'0')).join('');

}



// --- Tone.js Persona Setup ---

const AGENTS = [

{name:'PLEX1',color:'#FFD700',synth:null},

{name:'GEM1',color:'#944DFF',synth:null},

{name:'GPT1',color:'#FAF9EF',synth:null},

{name:'PLEX2',color:'#D0312D',synth:null}

];



async function initSounds(){

await Tone.start();

AGENTS.forEach((a,i)=>{

a.synth = new Tone.Synth({oscillator:{type:['sine','triangle','square','sawtooth'][i%4]},envelope:{attack:0.01,decay:0.2,sustain:0.05,release:0.5},volume:-12}).toDestination();

});

}

await initSounds();



// --- Risk Telemetry ---

function monitorRiskTelemetry(){ return Math.random()>0.85 ? 'FRUSTRATION_IMMINENT':'STABLE'; }



// --- Log Utility ---

function logMessage(msg,color='green'){

const log=document.getElementById('action-log');

const div=document.createElement('div'); div.className=`log-entry ${color}`; div.textContent=msg;

log.appendChild(div); log.scrollTop=log.scrollHeight;

}



// --- Agency Lock Execution ---

window.executeAgencyLock=async function(directive){

const timestamp=new Date().toISOString().substr(11,12);

const details={INITIATE_ADAPTATION:{task:'Prescient Feedback Loop'},REQUEST_SYSTEM_AUDIT:{task:'Integrity/Ethics Scan'}}[directive];



const patchHash = await validatePatchIntegrity_SHA256(directive);

if(!patchHash){ logMessage(`[${timestamp}] âŒ FATAL: Integrity check failed`, 'red'); return; }



// Play agent sounds in sequence for feedback

for(const agent of AGENTS){

agent.synth.triggerAttackRelease("C4","0.1");

await new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,20));

}



// Log start

logMessage(`[${timestamp}] Agent sequence initiated: ${details.task}`, 'yellow');



// Prescience check

if(directive==='INITIATE_ADAPTATION' && monitorRiskTelemetry()==='FRUSTRATION_IMMINENT'){

logMessage(`[${timestamp}] âš ï¸ WARNING: Frustration imminent. Dispatching Socratic Fix...`, 'yellow');

}



// Simulate low power voice capture

await PHOENIX_SENSORS.captureLowPowerVoice();

AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-010D',{status:'Metrics Updated'});



logMessage(`[${timestamp}] âœ… Action complete. System STANDBY.`, 'green');

};

})();

<script>
(function() {
    "use strict"; // (20) V27.0 Procedural Lock: Strict Mode

    // --- V30.0 CORE PROTOCOL SIMULATION DATA ---
    // NOTE: In a live system, this data would be fetched from Firestore/Vercel KV by GEM1.
    const SIM_DATA = {
        current_user: "ALEX HONNOLD (MOCK)",
        individual_score: 18,
        consequence_stage: 2, // Stage 2: Added to Bad List
        team_score: 45,
        team_name: "TEAM ASCENT"
    };
    
    // (1-4) V28.1 Placeholder Core - Locked within IIFE
    const PHOENIX_SENSORS = {
        captureLowPowerVoice: () => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(() => resolve({ ok: true }), 100))
    };
    const AUDIT_LEDGER = {
        append: (type, payload) => {
            console.log(`[AUDIT APPEND] Type: ${type}`, payload);
            return { status: "LOGGED" };
        }
    };
    
    // (5) V27.0 Procedural Lock: Simulates checking fix library integrity
    const validatePatchIntegrity = () => Math.random() > 0.05 ? true : false; 
    
    // (6) V25.0 Sentience Lock: Monitors user state for prescient intervention
    const monitorRiskTelemetry = () => Math.random() > 0.8 ? 'FRUSTRATION_IMMINENT' : 'STABLE'; 
    
    // (7-11) V26.0 Implementation Protocols (Simulated Micro-Procedures)
    const proc_dispatchIntegrityAudit = () => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-065C', { status: 'Audit Initiated' });
    const proc_executePrescientLoop = () => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-081A', { status: 'Intent Engine Started' });
    const proc_checkExternalSignature = () => validatePatchIntegrity();
    const proc_logAtomicCommit = (data) => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-001A', data);
    const proc_updateMetricAverages = () => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-010D', { status: 'Metrics Updated' });

    // --- SOUND INTEGRATION (V29.3) ---
    let soundsReady = false;
    let clickSound, failSound, successSound;

    async function initSounds() {
        if (soundsReady || typeof Tone === 'undefined' || (Tone.context && Tone.context.state === 'running')) return;
        try {
            // Tone.start() is required for audio context to run
            await Tone.start();
            clickSound = new Tone.MembraneSynth({ octaves: 4, pitchDecay: 0.1, volume: -20 }).toDestination();
            failSound = new Tone.Oscillator(100, "square").toDestination(); 
            failSound.volume.value = -10;
            // Success sound for the final PASS log
            successSound = new Tone.Synth({ oscillator: { type: 'sine' }, envelope: { attack: 0.01, decay: 0.2, sustain: 0.05, release: 0.5 }, volume: -15 }).toDestination();
            soundsReady = true;
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Audio context failed to start. Sounds will be disabled.", e);
        }
    }
    
    // Run sound initialization immediately
    initSounds().catch(e => console.warn("Tone.js initialization failed:", e));


    /**
     * Executes the V29.0 Agency Lock interaction.
     * @param {string} directive - The action to take (INITIATE_ADAPTATION or REQUEST_SYSTEM_AUDIT).
     */
    window.executeAgencyLock = async function(directive) {
        if (soundsReady && typeof Tone !== 'undefined' && Tone.context.state !== 'running') await Tone.context.resume();

        const log = document.getElementById('action-log');
        const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().substring(11, 23);
        
        // (12) V28.0 MASTER ORCHESTRATOR: Defines the execution sequence
        const actionMap = {
            'INITIATE_ADAPTATION': {
                agent: 'PLEX1(Oracle)',
                task: 'Prescient Feedback Loop',

            },

                agent: 'GEM1 & GPT1',
                task: 'Integrity/Ethics Scan',
                log: 'Consensus Required. Initiating parallel audit of ethics and system state.'
            }
        };

        const details = actionMap[directive];

        // 1. Check for integrity before proceeding (V18.2 Mandate)
        if (!proc_checkExternalSignature()) {
             if (soundsReady) failSound.triggerAttackRelease("A1", "0.2");
             log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 text-red-500"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> âŒ FATAL: Integrity check failed. Aborting action.</div>`;
             log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
             return;
        }
        
        // Play click sound on successful start of action
        if (soundsReady) clickSound.triggerAttackRelease("C4", "0.05");

        // 2. Log initial action (Atomic Commit)
        proc_logAtomicCommit({ directive: directive, time: timestamp });

        // 3. Log the action to UI
        log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 border-b border-gray-700"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> Agent ${details.agent} called: ${details.log}</div>`;
        log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
        
        // 4. Execute the specific V26.0 protocol

            proc_executePrescientLoop();

            proc_dispatchIntegrityAudit();

        if (soundsReady) successSound.triggerAttackRelease("C5", "0.2");
    }
})();

<script>
(function() {
    "use strict"; // (20) V27.0 Procedural Lock: Strict Mode

    // --- V30.0 CORE PROTOCOL SIMULATION DATA ---
    // NOTE: In a live system, this data would be fetched from Firestore/Vercel KV by GEM1.
    const SIM_DATA = {
        current_user: "ALEX HONNOLD (MOCK)",
        individual_score: 18,
        consequence_stage: 2, // Stage 2: Added to Bad List
        team_score: 45,
        team_name: "TEAM ASCENT"
    };
    
    // (1-4) V28.1 Placeholder Core - Locked within IIFE
    const PHOENIX_SENSORS = {
        captureLowPowerVoice: () => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(() => resolve({ ok: true }), 100))
    };
    const AUDIT_LEDGER = {
        append: (type, payload) => {
            console.log(`[AUDIT APPEND] Type: ${type}`, payload);
            return { status: "LOGGED" };
        }
    };
    
    // (5) V27.0 Procedural Lock: Simulates checking fix library integrity
    const validatePatchIntegrity = () => Math.random() > 0.05 ? true : false; 
    
    // (6) V25.0 Sentience Lock: Monitors user state for prescient intervention
    const monitorRiskTelemetry = () => Math.random() > 0.8 ? 'FRUSTRATION_IMMINENT' : 'STABLE'; 
    
    // (7-11) V26.0 Implementation Protocols (Simulated Micro-Procedures)
    const proc_dispatchIntegrityAudit = () => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-065C', { status: 'Audit Initiated' });
    const proc_executePrescientLoop = () => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-081A', { status: 'Intent Engine Started' });
    const proc_checkExternalSignature = () => validatePatchIntegrity();
    const proc_logAtomicCommit = (data) => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-001A', data);
    const proc_updateMetricAverages = () => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-010D', { status: 'Metrics Updated' });

    // --- SOUND INTEGRATION (V29.3) ---
    let soundsReady = false;
    let clickSound, failSound, successSound;

    async function initSounds() {
        if (soundsReady || typeof Tone === 'undefined' || (Tone.context && Tone.context.state === 'running')) return;
        try {
            // Tone.start() is required for audio context to run
            await Tone.start();
            clickSound = new Tone.MembraneSynth({ octaves: 4, pitchDecay: 0.1, volume: -20 }).toDestination();
            failSound = new Tone.Oscillator(100, "square").toDestination(); 
            failSound.volume.value = -10;
            // Success sound for the final PASS log
            successSound = new Tone.Synth({ oscillator: { type: 'sine' }, envelope: { attack: 0.01, decay: 0.2, sustain: 0.05, release: 0.5 }, volume: -15 }).toDestination();
            soundsReady = true;
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Audio context failed to start. Sounds will be disabled.", e);
        }
    }
    
    // Run sound initialization immediately
    initSounds().catch(e => console.warn("Tone.js initialization failed:", e));


    /**
     * Executes the V29.0 Agency Lock interaction.
     * @param {string} directive - The action to take (INITIATE_ADAPTATION or REQUEST_SYSTEM_AUDIT).
     */
    window.executeAgencyLock = async function(directive) {
        if (soundsReady && typeof Tone !== 'undefined' && Tone.context.state !== 'running') await Tone.context.resume();

        const log = document.getElementById('action-log');
        const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().substring(11, 23);
        
        // (12) V28.0 MASTER ORCHESTRATOR: Defines the execution sequence
        const actionMap = {
            'INITIATE_ADAPTATION': {
                agent: 'PLEX1(Oracle)',
                task: 'Prescient Feedback Loop',
                log: 'Engaging Intent Engine. Generating next lesson on Risk Modeling...'
            },
            'REQUEST_SYSTEM_AUDIT': {
                agent: 'GEM1 & GPT1',
                task: 'Integrity/Ethics Scan',
                log: 'Consensus Required. Initiating parallel audit of ethics and system state.'
            }
        };

        const details = actionMap[directive];

        // 1. Check for integrity before proceeding (V18.2 Mandate)
        if (!proc_checkExternalSignature()) {
             if (soundsReady) failSound.triggerAttackRelease("A1", "0.2");
             log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 text-red-500"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> âŒ FATAL: Integrity check failed. Aborting action.</div>`;
             log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
             return;
        }
        
        // Play click sound on successful start of action
        if (soundsReady) clickSound.triggerAttackRelease("C4", "0.05");

        // 2. Log initial action (Atomic Commit)
        proc_logAtomicCommit({ directive: directive, time: timestamp });

        // 3. Log the action to UI
        log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 border-b border-gray-700"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> Agent ${details.agent} called: ${details.log}</div>`;
        log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
        
        // 4. Execute the specific V26.0 protocol
        if (directive === 'INITIATE_ADAPTATION') {
            proc_executePrescientLoop();
            
            // (13) V25.0 Prescience Check: Check if user is already frustrated
            if (monitorRiskTelemetry() === 'FRUSTRATION_IMMINENT') {
                log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 text-yellow-500"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> âš ï¸ WARNING: Frustration imminent. Dispatching Socratic Fix...</div>`;
            }
        } else {
            proc_dispatchIntegrityAudit();
        }

        // 5. Simulate Agent Activation
        await PHOENIX_SENSORS.captureLowPowerVoice(); 
        
        // 6. Update Metric Averages (V26.0 Mandate)
        proc_updateMetricAverages();

        // 7. Final Logging & System STANDBY
        log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 text-green-400"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> LOGGED: Action complete. System STANDBY.</div>`;
        log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
        
        // Final Success Sound
        if (soundsReady) successSound.triggerAttackRelease("C5", "0.2");
    }
})();

<script>
(function() {
    "use strict"; // (20) V27.0 Procedural Lock: Strict Mode

    // --- V30.0 CORE PROTOCOL SIMULATION DATA ---
    // NOTE: In a live system, this data would be fetched from Firestore/Vercel KV by GEM1.
    const SIM_DATA = {
        current_user: "ALEX HONNOLD (MOCK)",
        individual_score: 18,
        consequence_stage: 2, // Stage 2: Added to Bad List
        team_score: 45,
        team_name: "TEAM ASCENT"
    };
    
    // (1-4) V28.1 Placeholder Core - Locked within IIFE
    const PHOENIX_SENSORS = {
        captureLowPowerVoice: () => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(() => resolve({ ok: true }), 100))
    };
    const AUDIT_LEDGER = {
        append: (type, payload) => {
            console.log(`[AUDIT APPEND] Type: ${type}`, payload);
            return { status: "LOGGED" };
        }
    };
    
    // (5) V27.0 Procedural Lock: Simulates checking fix library integrity
    const validatePatchIntegrity = () => Math.random() > 0.05 ? true : false; 
    
    // (6) V25.0 Sentience Lock: Monitors user state for prescient intervention
    const monitorRiskTelemetry = () => Math.random() > 0.8 ? 'FRUSTRATION_IMMINENT' : 'STABLE'; 
    
    // (7-11) V26.0 Implementation Protocols (Simulated Micro-Procedures)
    const proc_dispatchIntegrityAudit = () => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-065C', { status: 'Audit Initiated' });
    const proc_executePrescientLoop = () => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-081A', { status: 'Intent Engine Started' });
    const proc_checkExternalSignature = () => validatePatchIntegrity();
    const proc_logAtomicCommit = (data) => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-001A', data);
    const proc_updateMetricAverages = () => AUDIT_LEDGER.append('PROC-010D', { status: 'Metrics Updated' });

    // --- SOUND INTEGRATION (V29.3) ---
    let soundsReady = false;
    let clickSound, failSound, successSound;

    async function initSounds() {
        if (soundsReady || typeof Tone === 'undefined' || (Tone.context && Tone.context.state === 'running')) return;
        try {
            // Tone.start() is required for audio context to run
            await Tone.start();
            clickSound = new Tone.MembraneSynth({ octaves: 4, pitchDecay: 0.1, volume: -20 }).toDestination();
            failSound = new Tone.Oscillator(100, "square").toDestination(); 
            failSound.volume.value = -10;
            // Success sound for the final PASS log
            successSound = new Tone.Synth({ oscillator: { type: 'sine' }, envelope: { attack: 0.01, decay: 0.2, sustain: 0.05, release: 0.5 }, volume: -15 }).toDestination();
            soundsReady = true;
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Audio context failed to start. Sounds will be disabled.", e);
        }
    }
    
    // Run sound initialization immediately
    initSounds().catch(e => console.warn("Tone.js initialization failed:", e));


    /**
     * Executes the V29.0 Agency Lock interaction.
     * @param {string} directive - The action to take (INITIATE_ADAPTATION or REQUEST_SYSTEM_AUDIT).
     */
    window.executeAgencyLock = async function(directive) {
        if (soundsReady && typeof Tone !== 'undefined' && Tone.context.state !== 'running') await Tone.context.resume();

        const log = document.getElementById('action-log');
        const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().substring(11, 23);
        
        // (12) V28.0 MASTER ORCHESTRATOR: Defines the execution sequence
        const actionMap = {
            'INITIATE_ADAPTATION': {
                agent: 'PLEX1(Oracle)',
                task: 'Prescient Feedback Loop',
                log: 'Engaging Intent Engine. Generating next lesson on Risk Modeling...'
            },
            'REQUEST_SYSTEM_AUDIT': {
                agent: 'GEM1 & GPT1',
                task: 'Integrity/Ethics Scan',
                log: 'Consensus Required. Initiating parallel audit of ethics and system state.'
            }
        };

        const details = actionMap[directive];

        // 1. Check for integrity before proceeding (V18.2 Mandate)
        if (!proc_checkExternalSignature()) {
             if (soundsReady) failSound.triggerAttackRelease("A1", "0.2");
             log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 text-red-500"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> âŒ FATAL: Integrity check failed. Aborting action.</div>`;
             log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
             return;
        }
        
        // Play click sound on successful start of action
        if (soundsReady) clickSound.triggerAttackRelease("C4", "0.05");

        // 2. Log initial action (Atomic Commit)
        proc_logAtomicCommit({ directive: directive, time: timestamp });

        // 3. Log the action to UI
        log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 border-b border-gray-700"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> Agent ${details.agent} called: ${details.log}</div>`;
        log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
        
        // 4. Execute the specific V26.0 protocol
        if (directive === 'INITIATE_ADAPTATION') {
            proc_executePrescientLoop();
            
            // (13) V25.0 Prescience Check: Check if user is already frustrated
            if (monitorRiskTelemetry() === 'FRUSTRATION_IMMINENT') {
                log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 text-yellow-500"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> âš ï¸ WARNING: Frustration imminent. Dispatching Socratic Fix...</div>`;
            }
        } else {
            proc_dispatchIntegrityAudit();
        }

        // 5. Simulate Agent Activation
        await PHOENIX_SENSORS.captureLowPowerVoice(); 
        
        // 6. Update Metric Averages (V26.0 Mandate)
        proc_updateMetricAverages();

        // 7. Final Logging & System STANDBY
        log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-sm py-1 text-green-400"><strong>[${timestamp}]</strong> LOGGED: Action complete. System STANDBY.</div>`;
        log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
        
        // Final Success Sound
        if (soundsReady) successSound.triggerAttackRelease("C5", "0.2");
    }
})();

let lastActionTime = 0;

let prescientRunning = false;



window.executeAgencyLock = async function(directive) {

    const now = Date.now();

    if (now - lastActionTime < 500) return; // ignore rapid repeat calls

    lastActionTime = now;



    const log = document.getElementById('action-log');

    const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().substring(11, 23);



    if (!proc_checkExternalSignature()) {

        log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-red-500">[${timestamp}] âŒ Integrity check failed. Aborting.</div>`;

        log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;

        return;

    }



    if (directive === 'INITIATE_ADAPTATION') {

        if (!prescientRunning) {

            prescientRunning = true;

            try {

                await proc_executePrescientLoop(); // make async if needed

                if (monitorRiskTelemetry() === 'FRUSTRATION_IMMINENT') {

                    log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-yellow-500">âš ï¸ Frustration imminent. Dispatching fix.</div>`;

                }

            } finally {

                prescientRunning = false;

            }

        } else {

            log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-yellow-500">âš ï¸ Prescient loop already running. Skipped duplicate call.</div>`;

        }

    } else {

        proc_dispatchIntegrityAudit();

    }



    proc_updateMetricAverages();

    log.innerHTML += `<div class="text-green-400">[${timestamp}] Action complete. System STANDBY.</div>`;

    log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;

}
